                <img class="j-lazy-img" src="{{:~wbSettings.staticSiteUrl}}/i/blank.gif" data-original="{{:~ImageUrl(cod1S, ~root.imgType, ~root.imgIdx)}}" alt="{{> name}}">
                {{else}}
                <img src="{{:~ImageUrl(cod1S, ~root.imgType, ~root.imgIdx)}}" alt="{{> name}}">
                {{/if}}
                {{if ~root.fastView}}<button class="preview-item j-open-product-popup">Быстрый просмотр</button>{{/if}}
            <div class="label-only-adults">Товары для взрослых</div>
            </div>
            <div class="item-info">
                <div class="price-block j-price-block">
                {{include tmpl='priceTmpl' /}}
                </div>

                    <span class="good-brand">{{:brand}}</span> / <span class="good-name">{{:name}}</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </a>
    </div>
    {{/for}}
</script>
